1. The first image shows a solid gray circle.

A. Shows two blue shapes (a hexagon and a square) in the bottom half.
B. Shows two blue shapes (a hexagon and a square) in the bottom half, but they are smaller.
C. Shows two blue shapes (a hexagon and a square) in the bottom half, but they are larger.

Based on the sequence, the correct option should have the same shapes as the top half but reflected to the bottom half. Option A fits this description perfectly.
